local function load_enemy(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.TemplatedEnemyProxy(v["name"])
  proxy.based_on_enemy = v["based_on_enemy"]
  for k, weapon in ipairs(v["weapons"]) do
    proxy:AddWeapon(weapon)
  end
  if v["body_hit_points"] then
    proxy.body_hit_points = v["body_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["armor_hit_points"] then
    proxy.armor_hit_points = v["armor_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["shield_hit_points"] then
    proxy.shield_hit_points = v["shield_hit_points"]
  end
  proxy.xp = v["xp"] or 0
  proxy.base_score = v["score"] or -1

  local version = proxy.version
  if version == 2 then
    proxy.hull2 = v["hull2"]
    proxy.armor2 = v["armor2"]
    proxy.shield2 = v["shield2"]
    proxy.shield2_repair_time = 4
    proxy.critical_hit_damage_modifier = 1.5
    proxy.armor_damage_modifier = 0.70
    proxy.shield_damage_modifier = 2.5
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
end

local function load_enemies(enemies)
  for k, v in ipairs(enemies) do
    load_enemy(v)
  end
end

local function load_stage(data)
  local proxy = phoenix2.StageProxy(data["name"])
  proxy.background = data["background"]
  for k, v in ipairs(data["acts"]) do
    local act = phoenix2.ActSpec()
    for k2, v2 in ipairs(v["encounters"]) do
      local encounter = phoenix2.EncounterSpec()
      for k3, v3 in ipairs(v2["enemies"]) do
        local enemy = phoenix2.EnemySpec()
        enemy.name = v3["name"]
        enemy.destination = v3["destination"]
        local ellipse = v3["hover_ellipse"]
        if ellipse ~= nil then
          enemy.hover_ellipse = ellipse
        end
        encounter:AddEnemy(enemy)
      end
      act:AddEncounter(encounter)
    end
    act.zoom_scale = v["zoom_scale"] or 1.0
    if v["flavour_keyword"] ~= nil then
      act.flavour_keyword = v["flavour_keyword"]
    end
    proxy:AddAct(act)
  end

  if data["auto_respawn"] ~= nil then
    proxy.auto_respawn = data["auto_respawn"]
  end
  if data["energy_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.energy_reminder = data["energy_reminder"]
  end
  if data["emp_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.emp_reminder = data["emp_reminder"]
  end
  if data["laser_warning"] ~= nil then
    proxy.laser_warning = data["laser_warning"]
  end
  if data["reactor_infographic_wave"] ~= nil then
    if proxy.AddInfographic ~= nil then
      local infographic = phoenix2.InfographicSpec()
      infographic.name = "image.infographic.reactor"
      infographic.text = "prologue_only_hit_on_core"
      infographic.time = 1.2
      infographic.wave_index = data["reactor_infographic_wave"]
      proxy:AddInfographic(infographic)
    end
  end
  if data["reactor_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.reactor_reminder = data["reactor_reminder"]
  end


  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return data["name"]
end

local function load_weapon(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.WeaponProxy(v["name"])

  if v["animated_appearance"] ~= nil then
    proxy.animated_appearance = v["animated_appearance"]
  end

  proxy.color = { 255, 255, 1, 1 }
  if v["weapon_actions_name"] ~= nil then
    proxy.weapon_actions_name = v["weapon_actions_name"]
  end
  if v["weapon_actions_code"] ~= nil then
    proxy.lua_weapon_action_code = v["weapon_actions_code"]
  end

  proxy.damage_per_second = -1

  proxy.smart_aiming = v["smart_aiming"] or false
  proxy.projectile_speed = v["projectile_speed"] or 200

  local on_destruction = v["on_destruction"]
  if on_destruction ~= nil then
    local name = on_destruction["name"]
    local location = {0, 0}
    local orientation = {0, 1}
    local z_order = 0.0
    proxy:SetOnDestructionActor(name, location, orientation, z_order)
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return v["name"]
end

local function load_weapons(weapons)
  for k, v in ipairs(weapons) do
    load_weapon(v)
  end
end

-- Copyright 2024 Firi Games. All rights reserved.
--
-- @author phoenix2.generator
--
-- Stage generated on 2024-09-14

local function load_enemy(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.TemplatedEnemyProxy(v["name"])
  proxy.based_on_enemy = v["based_on_enemy"]
  for k, weapon in ipairs(v["weapons"]) do
    proxy:AddWeapon(weapon)
  end
  if v["body_hit_points"] then
    proxy.body_hit_points = v["body_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["armor_hit_points"] then
    proxy.armor_hit_points = v["armor_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["shield_hit_points"] then
    proxy.shield_hit_points = v["shield_hit_points"]
  end
  proxy.xp = v["xp"] or 0
  proxy.base_score = v["score"] or -1

  local version = proxy.version
  if version == 2 then
    proxy.hull2 = v["hull2"]
    proxy.armor2 = v["armor2"]
    proxy.shield2 = v["shield2"]
    proxy.shield2_repair_time = 4
    proxy.critical_hit_damage_modifier = 1.5
    proxy.armor_damage_modifier = 0.70
    proxy.shield_damage_modifier = 2.5
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
end

local function load_enemies(enemies)
  for k, v in ipairs(enemies) do
    load_enemy(v)
  end
end

local function load_stage(data)
  local proxy = phoenix2.StageProxy(data["name"])
  proxy.background = data["background"]
  for k, v in ipairs(data["acts"]) do
    local act = phoenix2.ActSpec()
    for k2, v2 in ipairs(v["encounters"]) do
      local encounter = phoenix2.EncounterSpec()
      for k3, v3 in ipairs(v2["enemies"]) do
        local enemy = phoenix2.EnemySpec()
        enemy.name = v3["name"]
        enemy.destination = v3["destination"]
        local ellipse = v3["hover_ellipse"]
        if ellipse ~= nil then
          enemy.hover_ellipse = ellipse
        end
        encounter:AddEnemy(enemy)
      end
      act:AddEncounter(encounter)
    end
    act.zoom_scale = v["zoom_scale"] or 1.0
    if v["flavour_keyword"] ~= nil then
      act.flavour_keyword = v["flavour_keyword"]
    end
    proxy:AddAct(act)
  end

  if data["auto_respawn"] ~= nil then
    proxy.auto_respawn = data["auto_respawn"]
  end
  if data["energy_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.energy_reminder = data["energy_reminder"]
  end
  if data["emp_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.emp_reminder = data["emp_reminder"]
  end
  if data["laser_warning"] ~= nil then
    proxy.laser_warning = data["laser_warning"]
  end
  if data["reactor_infographic_wave"] ~= nil then
    if proxy.AddInfographic ~= nil then
      local infographic = phoenix2.InfographicSpec()
      infographic.name = "image.infographic.reactor"
      infographic.text = "prologue_only_hit_on_core"
      infographic.time = 1.2
      infographic.wave_index = data["reactor_infographic_wave"]
      proxy:AddInfographic(infographic)
    end
  end
  if data["reactor_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.reactor_reminder = data["reactor_reminder"]
  end


  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return data["name"]
end

local function load_weapon(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.WeaponProxy(v["name"])

  if v["animated_appearance"] ~= nil then
    proxy.animated_appearance = v["animated_appearance"]
  end

  proxy.color = { 255, 255, 1, 1 }
  if v["weapon_actions_name"] ~= nil then
    proxy.weapon_actions_name = v["weapon_actions_name"]
  end
  if v["weapon_actions_code"] ~= nil then
    proxy.lua_weapon_action_code = v["weapon_actions_code"]
  end

  proxy.damage_per_second = -1

  proxy.smart_aiming = v["smart_aiming"] or false
  proxy.projectile_speed = v["projectile_speed"] or 200

  local on_destruction = v["on_destruction"]
  if on_destruction ~= nil then
    local name = on_destruction["name"]
    local location = {0, 0}
    local orientation = {0, 1}
    local z_order = 0.0
    proxy:SetOnDestructionActor(name, location, orientation, z_order)
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return v["name"]
end

local function load_weapons(weapons)
  for k, v in ipairs(weapons) do
    load_weapon(v)
  end
end

-- Copyright 2024 Firi Games. All rights reserved.
--
-- @author phoenix2.generator
--
-- Stage generated on 2024-09-14
--

local function load_enemy(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.TemplatedEnemyProxy(v["name"])
  proxy.based_on_enemy = v["based_on_enemy"]
  for k, weapon in ipairs(v["weapons"]) do
    proxy:AddWeapon(weapon)
  end
  if v["body_hit_points"] then
    proxy.body_hit_points = v["body_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["armor_hit_points"] then
    proxy.armor_hit_points = v["armor_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["shield_hit_points"] then
    proxy.shield_hit_points = v["shield_hit_points"]
  end
  proxy.xp = v["xp"] or 0
  proxy.base_score = v["score"] or -1

  local version = proxy.version
  if version == 2 then
    proxy.hull2 = v["hull2"]
    proxy.armor2 = v["armor2"]
    proxy.shield2 = v["shield2"]
    proxy.shield2_repair_time = 4
    proxy.critical_hit_damage_modifier = 1.5
    proxy.armor_damage_modifier = 0.70
    proxy.shield_damage_modifier = 2.5
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
end

local function load_enemies(enemies)
  for k, v in ipairs(enemies) do
    load_enemy(v)
  end
end

local function load_stage(data)
  local proxy = phoenix2.StageProxy(data["name"])
  proxy.background = data["background"]
  for k, v in ipairs(data["acts"]) do
    local act = phoenix2.ActSpec()
    for k2, v2 in ipairs(v["encounters"]) do
      local encounter = phoenix2.EncounterSpec()
      for k3, v3 in ipairs(v2["enemies"]) do
        local enemy = phoenix2.EnemySpec()
        enemy.name = v3["name"]
        enemy.destination = v3["destination"]
        local ellipse = v3["hover_ellipse"]
        if ellipse ~= nil then
          enemy.hover_ellipse = ellipse
        end
        encounter:AddEnemy(enemy)
      end
      act:AddEncounter(encounter)
    end
    act.zoom_scale = v["zoom_scale"] or 1.0
    if v["flavour_keyword"] ~= nil then
      act.flavour_keyword = v["flavour_keyword"]
    end
    proxy:AddAct(act)
  end

  if data["auto_respawn"] ~= nil then
    proxy.auto_respawn = data["auto_respawn"]
  end
  if data["energy_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.energy_reminder = data["energy_reminder"]
  end
  if data["emp_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.emp_reminder = data["emp_reminder"]
  end
  if data["laser_warning"] ~= nil then
    proxy.laser_warning = data["laser_warning"]
  end
  if data["reactor_infographic_wave"] ~= nil then
    if proxy.AddInfographic ~= nil then
      local infographic = phoenix2.InfographicSpec()
      infographic.name = "image.infographic.reactor"
      infographic.text = "prologue_only_hit_on_core"
      infographic.time = 1.2
      infographic.wave_index = data["reactor_infographic_wave"]
      proxy:AddInfographic(infographic)
    end
  end
  if data["reactor_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.reactor_reminder = data["reactor_reminder"]
  end


  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return data["name"]
end

local function load_weapon(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.WeaponProxy(v["name"])

  if v["animated_appearance"] ~= nil then
    proxy.animated_appearance = v["animated_appearance"]
  end

  proxy.color = { 255, 255, 1, 1 }
  if v["weapon_actions_name"] ~= nil then
    proxy.weapon_actions_name = v["weapon_actions_name"]
  end
  if v["weapon_actions_code"] ~= nil then
    proxy.lua_weapon_action_code = v["weapon_actions_code"]
  end

  proxy.damage_per_second = -1

  proxy.smart_aiming = v["smart_aiming"] or false
  proxy.projectile_speed = v["projectile_speed"] or 200

  local on_destruction = v["on_destruction"]
  if on_destruction ~= nil then
    local name = on_destruction["name"]
    local location = {0, 0}
    local orientation = {0, 1}
    local z_order = 0.0
    proxy:SetOnDestructionActor(name, location, orientation, z_order)
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return v["name"]
end

local function load_weapons(weapons)
  for k, v in ipairs(weapons) do
    load_weapon(v)
  end
end

-- @author phoenix2.generator

local function load_enemy(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.TemplatedEnemyProxy(v["name"])
  proxy.based_on_enemy = v["based_on_enemy"]
  for k, weapon in ipairs(v["weapons"]) do
    proxy:AddWeapon(weapon)
  end
  if v["body_hit_points"] then
    proxy.body_hit_points = v["body_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["armor_hit_points"] then
    proxy.armor_hit_points = v["armor_hit_points"]
  end
  if v["shield_hit_points"] then
    proxy.shield_hit_points = v["shield_hit_points"]
  end
  proxy.xp = v["xp"] or 0
  proxy.base_score = v["score"] or -1

  local version = proxy.version
  if version == 2 then
    proxy.hull2 = v["hull2"]
    proxy.armor2 = v["armor2"]
    proxy.shield2 = v["shield2"]
    proxy.shield2_repair_time = 4
    proxy.critical_hit_damage_modifier = 1.5
    proxy.armor_damage_modifier = 0.70
    proxy.shield_damage_modifier = 2.5
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
end

local function load_enemies(enemies)
  for k, v in ipairs(enemies) do
    load_enemy(v)
  end
end

local function load_stage(data)
  local proxy = phoenix2.StageProxy(data["name"])
  proxy.background = data["background"]
  for k, v in ipairs(data["acts"]) do
    local act = phoenix2.ActSpec()
    for k2, v2 in ipairs(v["encounters"]) do
      local encounter = phoenix2.EncounterSpec()
      for k3, v3 in ipairs(v2["enemies"]) do
        local enemy = phoenix2.EnemySpec()
        enemy.name = v3["name"]
        enemy.destination = v3["destination"]
        local ellipse = v3["hover_ellipse"]
        if ellipse ~= nil then
          enemy.hover_ellipse = ellipse
        end
        encounter:AddEnemy(enemy)
      end
      act:AddEncounter(encounter)
    end
    act.zoom_scale = v["zoom_scale"] or 1.0
    if v["flavour_keyword"] ~= nil then
      act.flavour_keyword = v["flavour_keyword"]
    end
    proxy:AddAct(act)
  end

  if data["auto_respawn"] ~= nil then
    proxy.auto_respawn = data["auto_respawn"]
  end
  if data["energy_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.energy_reminder = data["energy_reminder"]
  end
  if data["emp_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.emp_reminder = data["emp_reminder"]
  end
  if data["laser_warning"] ~= nil then
    proxy.laser_warning = data["laser_warning"]
  end
  if data["reactor_infographic_wave"] ~= nil then
    if proxy.AddInfographic ~= nil then
      local infographic = phoenix2.InfographicSpec()
      infographic.name = "image.infographic.reactor"
      infographic.text = "prologue_only_hit_on_core"
      infographic.time = 1.2
      infographic.wave_index = data["reactor_infographic_wave"]
      proxy:AddInfographic(infographic)
    end
  end
  if data["reactor_reminder"] ~= nil then
    proxy.reactor_reminder = data["reactor_reminder"]
  end


  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return data["name"]
end

local function load_weapon(v)
  local proxy = phoenix2.WeaponProxy(v["name"])

  if v["animated_appearance"] ~= nil then
    proxy.animated_appearance = v["animated_appearance"]
  end

  proxy.color = { 255, 255, 1, 1 }
  if v["weapon_actions_name"] ~= nil then
    proxy.weapon_actions_name = v["weapon_actions_name"]
  end
  if v["weapon_actions_code"] ~= nil then
    proxy.lua_weapon_action_code = v["weapon_actions_code"]
  end

  proxy.damage_per_second = -1

  proxy.smart_aiming = v["smart_aiming"] or false
  proxy.projectile_speed = v["projectile_speed"] or 200

  local on_destruction = v["on_destruction"]
  if on_destruction ~= nil then
    local name = on_destruction["name"]
    local location = {0, 0}
    local orientation = {0, 1}
    local z_order = 0.0
    proxy:SetOnDestructionActor(name, location, orientation, z_order)
  end

  flare.load_proxy(proxy)
  return v["name"]
end

local function load_weapons(weapons)
  for k, v in ipairs(weapons) do
    load_weapon(v)
  end
end
